Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Thoughts on Reading History 227

— Zhou Ge

I don't know why myself, but recently I have become very interested in reading history. In a thin book, from the primitive tribal society to the recent so-called capitalist society, this long period of historical facts, although brief, has after all been shown to me in a hurried manner.

The first thing that makes me feel is that what is called history seems to be a realistic portrayal of human beings constantly killing each other. In the era of commercial capitalism, the killing of natives in the colonies was often counted in the tens of thousands. Furthermore, from the evolution of commercial capitalism, there is the historical fact of the "sheep eating people" in England. Further, there is the so-called "育天 massacre" in France in 1848. Under the cruelty of Jacques, 50,000 people were killed in five days. … It makes me feel, what is the difference between humans and beasts?

The second thing that makes me feel is that every major large-scale killing has ultimately made some progress in society. Blood and the evolution of society are inseparable. What else is there besides blood to demand the advancement of a society, to demand the further perfection of human happiness? One drop of blood shed is one step forward for society, and human happiness is more complete. The value of blood lies here.

The third thing that makes me feel is that I feel our own era. It turns out that we are also creating history. In future history, the number of people killed may be several times more than the past "50,000". It is not uncommon for a bomb to kill thousands of people, and the killing of poison gas is even more indescribable. … Although these things make me a little chilled, when I think that future generations will feel the same way when they read this period of history, that "blood is related to the evolution of society and the further perfection of human happiness," I am also pleased.

Yes, the fate that history gives us is like this, but on the contrary, we are creating an even more glorious history!

Night in Xiwei 228

— Ye Ge

—One of the Drifting Notes

Stepping into the thin city tower of Xiwei City, it was already close to the twilight of dusk.

This mountain city, which grew up in a remote area, is not so strange to me. Last spring, I rushed up the mountain with a load of foreign goods. I heard that the battle took place at Jieguaan Pavilion. I stayed here for a week or two. The area of this city is probably less than three square miles, but there are four streets in the east, west, north, and south that are not so monotonous. The streets are filled with horse manure all year round. Dead rats, meat bones, and some piles of garbage that make people feel unpleasant at first sight.

I remembered that when I stayed here last year, I spent the night in a small inn at the bottom of Jitingjiao. It was opened by a young couple from Yongchun. The accommodation was cheap and the service was attentive. Why not go there to stay again? So, I went straight to Jitingjiao. Everything in Jitingjiao was as before, but the inn named "Daxing Inn," which was hung with a red paper and crookedly written, was gone. I was suspicious and thought I had gone the wrong way, so I ran back and forth on the street.

At the door of a tile house, I felt someone greeting me from behind from a distance. I turned around and saw a middle-aged woman with a high-heeled head and a black gown and trousers coming out from a door with a bamboo curtain, smiling and softly asking:

"Are you looking for a place to stay?" I nodded, and then I heard her say, "Daxing Inn has been closed for some time. Although we don't have a sign, we are the same as them!" Seeing that the evening was already deep, and she also seemed to be a business person, I agreed and followed her in.

This is a three-section tile house, which is obviously empty because no one has been moving for a long time. She took me to a guest room and then excused herself to go to the kitchen to cook water for me to wash my feet. After taking off the burden from my back and taking off the straw shoes on my feet that were covered with yellow dust, I really felt too tired. Lying on the bed, I felt a little drowsy.

At this time, the night had become dark, and the gray darkness filled the empty surroundings. Suddenly, I heard a tired cry of a baby, faintly coming from the kitchen, followed by a burst of dry coughs and muttering, which made me feel terrified and suspicious. I secretly got up from the bed and peered out through the glass on the bamboo window. In the mysterious blur, I found a pale monster wriggling in the dark. My heart was grabbed by a feeling of terror and beating. But when I looked closely, I understood everything. At this time, the monster was gradually groping over, and the crutches were hitting the ground, making clear sounds. Finally, he groped into my room and timidly asked in a soft voice, "Guest, has Ah Bei's mother not come to add fire here yet?" I replied that it didn't matter, and it was very suitable to rest in the dark.

"She is really too busy. She has to entertain guests and take care of her sick child; but what can be done! Since the Quanzhou-Xiwei car road opened last year, we can't afford to hire a partner. You, the guest, of course, know that the passing guests all take the main road, which is close and convenient. It's just hard for us business people. Just take the 'Daxing' inn in Jitingjiao, for example. It went bankrupt because it couldn't maintain its business. …" After the old man finished speaking, he sighed softly and fell silent. After a while, he groped in his pocket for a long time before taking out a box of self-lighting fire, and told me to light the lamp, the oil lamp was on the bed frame. I scratched a self-lighting fire and found the oil lamp and lit it. The spark flickered weakly for a while, and then slowly brightened. At this time, I realized that he was originally a blind man.

"Uncle, you must be over seventy this year!" I asked him:

"What's the use of being over seventy? When a person gets old, they have nothing. As the saying goes, a broken straw shoe plugs the table leg, and a broken straw shoe also has its use, but a disabled old man is useless. He eats three meals a day and waits to die! …" He was very excited, and his tone stirred him slightly, and his blind eyes flickered under the light. At this time, the middle-aged woman with the high-heeled head had come out and said that the water was boiled and asked me to go in and wash. So I took out a pair of cloth shoes from the bag and followed her in, and the old man sat on the edge of the bed thinking silently.

When I came out after washing my hands and feet, the old man had already groped out of the room with his crutches. In the middle of the night, I was suddenly awakened by a noise. After listening carefully, I realized that it was coming from the kitchen. There was a voice that seemed to be that of the middle-aged woman, shouting:

"You heartless ghost, do you still want to hide it? There will be no rice tomorrow, and Ah Bei has to see a doctor"...

"Ah Bei's mother, there is only this little bit in the bag! ..." The old man timidly defended, followed by a silence.

This woke me up from my dream. I thought I had been stolen, so I lit the lamp and secretly got up from the bed, opened the bag to see, and realized that the bag of copper coins was gone.

I managed to get through the night. The next morning, I was leaving early. The blind old man also specially sent me out with his crutches, and begged me in a close tone: "Guest, when you pass by next time, stop by and sit down! …"

Third-Class Prostitutes 229

— Guo Ka

—One of the Qingdao Scenery—

One summer, by a chance opportunity, I avoided the scorching heat of the whole summer next to a factory in Qingdao Dongzhen. The reason for using the word "避暑" (avoid the heat) here is entirely due to the associative effect of habit, because Qingdao has a special relationship with the concept of "避暑" like Qinhuangdao and Beidaihe. However, if you say that you are avoiding the heat in Qingdao Dongzhen, people who are familiar with this place may secretly laugh, because this place is completely under the shelter of some factory chimneys, the houses are short, the air is noisy, and the people who live here may not have a good mood to "avoid the heat".

Speaking of me living here, most of the daytime is spent in the stuffy cabin, listening to the roar of the big machines in a nearby beer factory: in the evening, after dinner, the weather is often half-bright and half-dark, like being covered with a piece of light gray yarn, everything is hazy and quiet, at this time, I often go to the road to wander because my stomach is a little full after dinner. This is the most comfortable time of the day.

One evening, when I was wandering aimlessly on the road with a friend who lived with me, he suddenly said:

"Let's go, I'll take you to a fresh place to stroll around."

"Where are you going?"

"You don't have to worry about it, you haven't seen it anyway."

I could only follow him curiously, thinking: such a factory area, besides friends in short clothes, are still friends in short clothes, what new toys can there be?

After walking for a long time on a road with sparse electric lights and a bit of fishy and sweaty smell, we ended up on a narrow street paved with pebbles. On both sides of the street were completely short bungalows. Each door had a round door lamp, and each lamp had an eye-catching small red character: "Third-Class Prostitute" Under the lamp, the first thing that came into my eyes was a pale white face. No matter how much this face was concealed by powder, it could not cover up the haggardness and aging, high cheekbones, sharp chin, and it looked like it was in its forties. When I saw people, I still smiled, but how terrible that kind of smile was! Under the dark silhouette, it looked like a gloomy ghost!

I curiously peeped forward, and there were such shadows under each lamp, some were lonely, some were in a pile of four or five; red pants, powdered faces, some looked like little girls who had just come from the countryside, with bound feet and combed small braids, and there was an unnatural smile on their gloomy faces. Some of the rooms were dark, and some could see a corner of a pink bedding from the window.

Yes, besides the terrible components, there is considerable seduction!

That friend quietly said meaningfully:

"This is the place. Haven't been here before, have you?"

This is definitely the first time I have been to this place! The street is dirty and uneven, and there is a burst of unpleasant smell, and often you will step on some wet things under your feet. Many workers are wandering around, they are bare-chested, tilted with cigarettes, and their eyes are glancing sideways to both sides.

In front of a door, there was a woman over middle age, - that's probably the procuress? - tall, with a cake face, and raised a pair of cow horn-like big feet that were more than half a foot long, patting the back of a worker's head and shouting:

"Ha child, you're here!" She then turned her head and shouted to those monster-like women, "Quick, quick!"

So the worker was swarmed into the small house.

Before this scene was finished, that friend suddenly pouted his chin and said:

"Look!"

In front of us, a little girl of fifteen or sixteen years old was twisting and pulling the corner of a worker's clothes. The worker was deliberately teasing her, and several people beside him shouted: "Good!"

Hearing this sound makes people feel horrified!

As a result, we left there with a horrified mood. After walking a long road silently, I re-asked that friend:

"What is this place called?"

"Third-class prostitutes, - that is, what is said (lowly)! A dozen copper plates can drink tea, and a few cents can do it once."

After a while, he said again:

"If you have the courage, I'll take you in to see it again one day."

I didn't answer him, I didn't know what to say.

Nonsense 230

— (Fool)

Through the efforts of Ambassador Arimasa, who returned to China yesterday, cherry seedlings were sent to China from Yokohama today on the Rokko Maru as a symbol of Sino-Japanese friendship. The city of Tokyo donated 5,000 branches to Nanjing and 500 branches to Shanghai. Tan Lao San said that Japan had forcibly occupied the four northeastern provinces and wanted to take the five northern provinces. Are these 5,500 seedlings the reward for the nine provinces? It is really absurd. I wonder how the brilliant Japanese diplomats came up with it. Or, it has another meaning, wanting to turn Nanjing and Shanghai into cherry blossom cities.

The new auxiliary coins have just come out, and counterfeit auxiliary coins have already been discovered. Tan Lao San said that I admire their agility in taking advantage of the situation, but the serious disruption of the new auxiliary currency system has unfolded before our eyes, which is a difficult thing.

Pen 231

— Hua Mu

Isn't it? In this world, what is worthy of my gratitude and has given me endless warmth and comfort is this pen. Since I took it in my hand from a small rectangular box, I have seen its weight, and my dim and dull life has suddenly become rich and active. I take it with me, drifting and wandering all over the world, and never let it leave the messy desk for a day or an evening, let it lie quietly, with fiery enthusiasm, on it, accompanied by ink bottles, pieces of paper, books, lonely years, and sad and happy life. On stormy nights, after crying and laughing, how sincere, gentle, and considerate it is, writing out for me

Page 20

The words that I love to read and are moved by... Can I not be moved? In this world, there is no second person who can treat me like it.

I also believe that it will never get tired. When it is put down from my hand, I secretly bless it in the quiet lamplight.

The Orange Seller 232

— Xu Da

"Papa, buy me a paper lantern, — a butterfly, prettier and bigger than last year's; and, and a string of 'hundred sons' firecrackers!..."

The little girl saw her father step over the threshold, abandoned her companion A'gen, and limped towards her father, grabbing the corner of his rough cotton short coat, staring with two clear black eyes, murmuring incessantly.

Zhi Xingbo put down the heavy load on his shoulders, sat down on a small stool under the eaves, his mouth wide open, revealing a few broken teeth, panting heavily; he unbuttoned his cotton coat, took off the dilapidated felt hat from his head, fanning himself vigorously, sweat beads like countless grains of sand oozing from his forehead.

Thinking that the Lantern Festival was just around the corner, he should buy a paper lantern for his son and daughter, as he had promised. However... he saw the innocent look on his son's face and felt extremely sad, hanging his head in repentance.

His wife came out of the kitchen, her small, pointed feet seemingly unable to support the weight of her body, making it difficult for her to walk without a limp. She walked up to Zhi Xingbo, scrutinized the pile of orange-yellow tangerines at his feet, and asked hesitantly:

"Xingbo's dad, why haven't you gone to the early market yet?... Tomorrow, tomorrow is the Lantern Festival! Maybe the price of tangerines will be higher these days!" Her voice was so soft, a little unnatural, the words slowly and softly slipping out of her mouth.

Zhi Xingbo's ancestors had passed down a few acres of tangerine orchards. Since then, Zhi Xingbo had inherited the legacy of his ancestors, working hard all year round. Naturally, the family's annual expenses depended on the fruits of the tangerine trees in these few acres of orchards. Every winter, when the tangerine orchards were full of tangerines, hanging heavily and greenly on the branches, Zhi Xingbo always felt as happy and joyful as if he had raised a son! At the same time, he was afraid that small thieves would sneak into the orchard at night to steal his tangerines. Therefore, during this "tangerine winter" period, after he had finished his dinner, he put down his rice bowl, casually wiped the corners of his mouth, and quickly ran to the orchard alone to guard it, braving the frost, dew, wind, and rain, bracing his spirits, walking alone in the middle of the night, shouldering a carrying pole, patrolling back and forth in the orchard. Especially when the year was coming to an end and the Lantern Festival was approaching, he defended so much that he even forgot about sleep.

In previous years, at this time, especially during the Lantern Festival, the price of tangerines was high, and he always had a large income to make up for the household expenses during the idle days after "tangerine winter".

"Why didn't I go to the early market? Cough, cough..." After clearing his throat, he took out his pipe from his waistband, filled it with tobacco, lit a match, and puffed, two wisps of blue smoke puffing out of his nostrils, and then continued: "The tangerine situation isn't good this year. Each load of tangerines has to donate more than one dollar in taxes. Naturally, 'what comes from the sheep, goes to the sheep,' so the price of tangerines has to be raised. But this year, many Taiwanese tangerines have come to the market. These look like devils! It is said that they don't need to pay taxes and can circulate everywhere. Although their tangerine juice is not as good as ours, the surface color and shape are much prettier than ours, and the price is cheaper. How can our tangerines not be hit by this! Anyway, people buy tangerines in the first month of the year just to give to relatives and friends, to add some festivity!... Alas! This year's tangerine situation, it's over!..."

The sunlight was blocked by a dark cloud, and a shadow appeared under the eaves, dim and gloomy.

"Papa, buy me a paper lantern, big and pretty; and a string of 'hundred sons' firecrackers!" The little girl grabbed her father's coat again, mumbling.

"You little devil, what are you making a fuss about!" Her mother angrily tapped her on the head.

Zhi Xingbo slowly stood up, walked behind the shrine, took out the paper lantern he had bought last year, and brushed off the dust with his felt hat, saying, "Xiao Nan, Daddy will make you a new one with colorful paper strips."

At Zhai Jun 233

— Hua

It was already dusk when we arrived at Zhai Jun from Saigon.

Zhai Jun is a small town in Annam. Having become accustomed to the bustling street scenes of Saigon, the scenery of Zhai Jun seemed too simple and too shabby to us. A row of trees like mimosa swayed their long branches weakly, sending out a wave of the unique, wearying heat of the southern country. The two of us felt as if we had just climbed out of the water, our bodies soaked in sweat.

My companion was a businessman who had been away from Tangyou for eighteen years. He was a man who believed in fate, a thorough fatalist. Under the malicious manipulation of the god of fate, for more than a decade, he had been constantly overwhelmed by poverty and suffering. It is said that when the rubber plantations in Singapore were making profits, he had also made a small fortune, but he eventually lost it gambling. Because he believed in fate, he would go to the casino, whether it was one "dong," one "xian," or even just one "bo" (he had been to Siam and Singapore). Having him as a companion on the long journey in a foreign country really reduced my loneliness and trouble. We met at a wholesale bureau in Saigon.

Now he was taking off the wide-brimmed straw hat from his head, constantly fanning himself. Rows of sweat flew down from the edge of the hat, and the black silk edge of the straw hat was also soaked with cold sweat. In some places, it was dried by the hot sun, and curved white salt ash floated up.

"We need to rest. In this weather, it would be really lucky not to get 'black dog sha.' What do you say?" He said.

I nodded. There were few pedestrians on the street. Many women with bare upper bodies sat outside their houses enjoying the cool air, rows of sweat beads oozing from their dark backs like soybeans. A small merchant selling shaved ice squatted by the roadside with his tall basket, already fast asleep. When I walked past him, I saw that he was drenched all over, and a long stream of saliva trailed from the corner of his mouth. Those dark-faced, thick-lipped native children, pressing their hands on their bulging bellies, looked at us in surprise, tugging at their mothers' skirts, and speaking to us in a Chaozhou accent that was only 30% proficient:

"One Tangshan person, two Tangshan people..." (To be continued)

Ballad Singing 236

Xu Wenbi's Opening

Shiyin (1340) 10:00 AM to 11:00 AM

Opening "New Flower Moon Song"

The spring breeze of March brings the red of flowers. Hundreds of flowers dance in the shadow of the moon like a bow. I am, slowly walking among the flowers, smelling the moon, under the shadow, again passing the moon bridge and flower path. However, the moon turns to the eastern wall, and the flower shadows are chaotic. The flowers bloom in the northern garden, and the moonlight dissolves. The clouds break, and the moon peeps at the beauty of the flowers. Late at night, I sleep in the moon's brightness. Suddenly, I meet Chang'e in the moon, leaving the flower kingdom. Pomelo emerges from the flower garden, from the moon palace. I love her, the affectionate moon shines on the dew among the flowers. The understanding flowers sway in the wind under the moon. I love her, the spirit of the moon. The appearance of the flower. The moonlight and flower fragrance are the same. We are, returning the soul to the moon before the flowers with wine. Singing under the moon to face the flowers. Slowly beating the flower drum in the moon. Gently playing the moon shooting bow under the flowers. When the moon sets, I rely on the flowers to send wine. When the flowers wither, there is still the moon to urge makeup. I really hope that the moon will be round, and the flowers will be good, and they will never be scattered. Who knows, the moon will be missing, and the flowers will be withered, which is too sad. From then on, the endless hatred of spring flowers and autumn moon. The autumn moon and spring flowers' hatred are endless. The most unforgettable thing is that the bright moon and plum blossoms sleep with a fragrant moon, like cleanliness. The moon is like the spirit, and the flower is like the appearance. Until now, the fallen flowers have followed the moon waves. The remnant moon is still in the red of the flowers. Since ancient times, mirror flowers and water moon are generally all empty.

Lu Qiuxia's Double Pearl Phoenix

Zhongxi (1040) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening "Woman Cries for Aloeswood"

The autumn scene in August is fragrant with osmanthus. Amorous women laugh in their boudoirs. Only hear, the sound of cold insects outside the window is endless. The wind blows the purple bamboo rustling. The iron horse in front of the eaves rings. Lower my head. Thinking to myself. Thinking of my mother's handsome and talented man. I have not been married to my husband's family for half a month. The maid sends a letter into my room. Saying that my talented man is sick in bed. I am an incense table, a void worship. Pray to the heavens and the city gods. I only hope that he is safe and well. I have not been married to my husband's family for a month. It hurts me. I have cried several times and returned to life. My husband asks me why I am sad. I only say that the pain in my abdomen is the most difficult to bear. I should have come to the spirit to offer condolences. Only because I am not more than a month old as a new bride. It is inconvenient to offer condolences to the mourning hall. I have to secretly wear three points of mourning for you. I put a piece of linen on my chest. I don't wear red and green clothes. I wear two pieces of plain clothes. A pair of arched shoes on linen. I ask the maid to buy a piece of aloeswood. I carve my talented man's handsome and beautiful face. Wearing a haiqing, yellow belt. Red satin shoes with black satin trim. It is difficult for me to carve you. Pacing back and forth in the study. It is difficult for me to carve you. Opening your mouth to call me dear sister. It is difficult for me to carve you. Facing each other, playing chess, looking at the west wing hall. I have to harden my head and say goodbye to my talented man. When I get on the sedan chair, I cry sadly. Idle people only tell idle stories. Only saying that I can't drop my father and mother. How do they know, I can't drop the affectionate and righteous handsome and talented man. Talented man, I offer you during the day on the dressing table. At night, the blue gauze curtain is the lyric hall. There are so many sad things in the world. Other people's sadness is sad. My sadness is hidden in my belly.

Drama 238

Leidian Drama Society

Jiaotong (1300) 5:30 PM to 6:30 PM

Leader: Chen Yi

Broadcast: A Luk... Ma Ling

Perform: Yeliena Bobova Bu... Chen Xiang

One: Grigory Smirnov... Lin Fei

Fool

Yeliena Bobova is a young and beautiful widow with dimples. Because her husband passed away, she feels very negative about the world. She buries herself at home all day. Although the old servant Luk bitterly persuades her, he still cannot move her dead heart.

At this time, the landlord Grigory Smirnov happened to come to Popova to calculate her husband's old debt of 1,200 rubles in order to pay the interest on the agricultural bank, but unfortunately, her accountant went to the city and would not come back until the day after tomorrow. She had no choice but to tell him to come and collect it the day after tomorrow, but he could not agree because he had to declare bankruptcy immediately if he did not pay the interest tomorrow. At that time, one had to have the money today, and the other could not pay you back until the day after tomorrow. The two could not retreat, and they quarreled. Finally, both sides were willing to use pistols to solve the matter through a duel.

But when he was really about to duel, her charming eyes and the dimples on her beautiful face took away his anger and courage, and he naturally softened. Instead, he knelt in front of her and begged her to marry him. Although she was determined to remain a widow for her husband! Finally, she said "Yes! Definitely!" Such contradictions!

At that time, her heart was being fought by the reason of "chastity" and the emotion of agreeing to his proposal! In the end, reason could not defeat emotion and was subdued!

When Luk called the coachman, gardener, etc. to rescue, he and she were hugging and sharing a long sweet kiss! Luk could only shout out "Oh God!"

Thus ended this comedy.

Movie News

China Film Gengsu Society "Sightseeing Group" Travels to "Nanxiang" 239

— Yin Han

Departure scheduled for the 23rd

Since the China Film Gengsu Society started to extensively recruit male and female members the day before yesterday (the 16th), the number of people requesting membership has been exceptionally enthusiastic. The "Sightseeing Group," which is being carried out step by step, has been formally established. The address and date of the first travel destination have been decided to be Nanxiang for sightseeing on the 23rd (next Sunday). Photography equipment, banners, and other application items are being manufactured. It is reported that several groups in Nanxiang have sent letters welcoming and receiving them. Chang Shaobai will lead the departure, and Li Lin will be the leader, it is said.

"Lust"

It is said that the "sex beauty" blockbuster, which is not suitable for children to watch, is being shown by Guotai today.

Entertainment Weekly Issue 6 Published 240

Synthesizing various entertainment publications, "Entertainment Weekly," since its publication, has been praised by readers for its agility, accuracy, novel and exquisite compilation and printing. Volume 2, Issue 6 has been published today. The content is more exciting than before, and the compilation is even more beautiful and eye-catching. In addition to various beautiful photos, the texts such as "The Strength of the Backup Team Increases Sharply," "Xu Yahui Regains Freedom," "The Queen of Balls Showcases the Power of the Lion in a Difficult Journey," "The Future of Shirley Temple," "Yuan Yemei is No Match for the Barber," "A Quick Sketch of Anna May Wong Arriving in Shanghai," and "Anna May Wong's Lifelong Event" are all news that is not easily obtained by the outside world. Starting from this issue, a page of "Modern Ballroom Dancing Techniques" will be added to each issue, with detailed introductions to the "dance method," "footwork," and "posture" of the latest ballroom dances. Readers can study step by step and become self-taught. If you want to know more details, please buy it quickly. Each copy is still sold for five cents. For sample requests, please include five cents for postage and send it to Entertainment Weekly, No. 138 Nanjing Road, Shanghai.

Star Bi-Monthly Spring Flower Special Published 241

"Star Bi-Monthly," published by Star Film Company and distributed by Huawai He Yi Company, Volume 4, Issue 3, was published on the 16th. This issue is a special issue for Spring Flowers. The cover is Yan Yuekai, the protagonist of Spring Flowers, exquisitely printed in two colors, which is very beautiful. In terms of photos, there are the protagonists and signatures of Spring Flowers, Gao Zhanfei, Huang Naishuang, Zhu Qiuren, and more than a dozen photos of the director, photography, sound recording, set design, etc. of the film, as well as stills and photography work photos, which are all extremely valuable. In terms of comics, there are more than a dozen pieces such as Dong Liang's "The Flowers Bloom, She Comes," as well as Wu Cun's handbook, the original manuscript of the script and songs of Spring Flowers. In terms of text, there are Fan Yanqiao's "Under the Spring Snow," Wang Pingling's poem "Ode to Spring Flowers," He Xuan's "Thoughts After Watching Spring Flowers," Hu Xuezhi's "A Realistic Poem," Wu Cun's "Words of the Director," Ying Keyi's "New Experience Given to Me by Spring Flowers," Lu Yinkeng's "A Success in Sound Recording," Yang Jingxin's "About the Background of Spring Flowers," Xiao Ziqing's "Small Excerpts of Spring Flowers," Luo Ying's "The Imagery of Spring Flowers," and the music scores of Spring Flowers and Wild Flower Fragrance, etc. The price of this issue is six cents. All newsstands and major bookstores have them for sale.

A Collection of Recent News from Tianyi 242

"Flowers and Grasses" was written by Hong Shen. Hong is also very attentive to the filming of this film. He came to Tianyi the other day to participate in rehearsals.

"Flowers and Grasses" stills have been re-shot into 16-inch large prints, which are becoming increasingly clear and unusual.

Playwright Leng Bo, in addition to being responsible for rehearsing at Tianyi, also serves as a screenwriter.

Tianyi's newcomer, Yao Ping, has studied vocal music for many years. His male solo is very well-founded and can be regarded as a solo talent in the film industry!

Part of "Flowers and Grasses" that was filmed was screened in the screening room yesterday. The sound, light, and acting skills were excellent.

The new sound film "Two Brothers" is quietly waiting for public release.
